# Awesome LLM Interpretability

A curated paper table for large language model and foundation model interpretability, including mechanistic interpretability, circuits, attribution, probing, representation analysis, sparse autoencoders, rationale faithfulness, hallucination diagnosis, and multimodal model explanations.

- [Large-model interpretability papers](#paper-table)
- [Detailed per-paper reading notes](./paper_notes_001_200/INDEX.md)
- [Batch reading overview](./interpretability_reading_notes.md)

## Tag Description

- ![Venue](https://img.shields.io/badge/Venue-blue) conference, journal, workshop, technical report, or arXiv source.
- ![Object](https://img.shields.io/badge/Object-purple) model object or explanation target, such as LLM, MLLM, hidden state, reasoning, hallucination, or transformer.
- ![Position](https://img.shields.io/badge/Position-cyan) where the interpretability signal lives, such as activation, layer, token, circuit, behavior, or output.
- ![Method](https://img.shields.io/badge/Method-lightgrey) method or topic tag, such as mechanistic, attribution, probing, SAE, rationale, steering, lens, or evaluation.
- ![Usage](https://img.shields.io/badge/Usage-yellow) intended use case, such as analyze, explain, detect, control, or evaluate.
- ![Relation](https://img.shields.io/badge/Relation-yellowgreen) relevance to large-model interpretability: core or related.

## Quick Reading Map

- **Mechanistic interpretability / circuits:** start with rows tagged `Mechanistic`, `SAE`, `Lens`, and `Representation`.
- **Explanation faithfulness / attribution:** start with rows tagged `Attribution`, `Rationale`, and `Evaluation`.
- **Reasoning and hallucination:** start with rows whose objects include `Reasoning` or `Hallucination`.
- **Multimodal interpretability:** start with rows whose objects include `MLLM`.

## Notes

- The list is venue-prioritized and query-generated, then deduplicated by normalized title.
- The `Problem & Method` column is intentionally concise: sentence one states the interpretability problem; sentence two states the main method signal from the title/abstract.
- Detailed reading notes for papers 001-200 are stored as one Markdown file per paper under [`paper_notes_001_200/`](./paper_notes_001_200/).
